### Changes for: [dilatator pupillae](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0001608)

 * _Deleted_
    *  **-** [dilatator pupillae](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0001608) *[function notes](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBPROP_0000009)*  It is innervated by the sympathetic system, which acts by releasing noradrenaline, which acts on alpha1-receptors. Thus, when presented with a threatening stimuli that activates the fight-or-flight response, this innervation dilates the iris, thus temporarily letting more light reach the retina
 * _Added_
    *  **+** [dilatator pupillae](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0001608) **SubClassOf** [develops from](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/RO_0002202) **some** [neurectoderm](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0002346) { [source](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#source)=ISBN:0781772214 } 
    *  **+** [dilatator pupillae](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0001608) *[function notes](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBPROP_0000009)* It is innervated by the sympathetic system, which acts by releasing noradrenaline, which acts on alpha1-receptors. Thus, when presented with a threatening stimuli that activates the fight-or-flight response, this innervation dilates the iris, thus temporarily letting more light reach the retina

### Changes for: [dorsal root ganglion](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0000044)

 * _Deleted_
    *  **-** [dorsal root ganglion](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0000044) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* * Sensory ganglia located on the dorsal spinal roots within the vertebral column. The spinal ganglion cells are pseudounipolar. The single primary branch bifurcates sending a peripheral process to carry sensory information from the periphery and a central branch which relays that information to the spinal cord or brain. (MSH) * ganglion found on the posterior root of each spinal nerve, composed of the unipolar nerve cell bodies of the sensory neurons of the nerve. (CSP) { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=NIFSTD:birnlex_2596 } 
 * _Added_
    *  **+** [dorsal root ganglion](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/UBERON_0000044) *[definition](http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/IAO_0000115)* Sensory ganglia located on the dorsal spinal roots within the vertebral column. The spinal ganglion cells are pseudounipolar. The single primary branch bifurcates sending a peripheral process to carry sensory information from the periphery and a central branch which relays that information to the spinal cord or brain. (MSH) * ganglion found on the posterior root of each spinal nerve, composed of the unipolar nerve cell bodies of the sensory neurons of the nerve. (CSP) { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=NIFSTD:birnlex_2596 }

It divides the esophagus from the trachea.  It divides the foregut tube into the laryngotracheal tube ventrally and esophagus dorsally. Developmental abnormalities can lead to a tracheoesophageal fistula. { [database cross reference](http://www.geneontology.org/formats/oboInOwl#hasDbXref)=[http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tracheoesophageal_septum](http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tracheoesophageal_septum) }
